                               ====
                              </font>
                             </p>
                             <p align="left">
                              <font face="Times New Roman" size="4">
                               <strong>
                                MIDDLE EAST
                               </strong>
                              </font>
                             </p>
                             <p align="left">
                              <a href="https://sana.sy/en/?p=225876">
                               <font face="Times New Roman" size="4">
                                <strong>
                                 Russia 
															opposes Western 
															attempts to impose 
															sanctions on Syria
                                </strong>
                               </font>
                              </a>
                             </p>
                             <p align="left">
                              <font face="Times New Roman">
                               <font size="4">
                                Act 
															of war:
                               </font>
                               <font color="#FF0000" size="5">
                                <strong>
                                </strong>
                               </font>
                               <a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/israel-strikes-target-iranian-oil-bound-for-syria-11615492789">
                                <font color="#FF0000" size="5">
                                 <strong>
                                  Israeli 
															Attacks Iranian Oil 
															Bound for Syria
                                 </strong>
                                </font>
                               </a>
                               <font color="#FF0000" size="5">
                                <strong>
                                 :
                                </strong>
                               </font>
                               <font color="#FF0000" size="4">
                                <strong>
                                </strong>
                               </font>
                               <font size="4">
                                In 
															2019, three ships 
															carrying Iranian oil 
															were attacked. In 
															2020, six ships used 
															by Iran were 
															targeted.
                               </font>
                              </font>
                             </p>
                             <p align="left">
                              <font face="Times New Roman">
                               <font size="4">
                                Act 
															of war:
                               </font>
                               <a href="https://www.thedrive.com/the-war-zone/39734/israel-has-been-launching-clandestine-attacks-on-iranian-oil-tankers-and-other-ships-report">
                                <font size="5">
                                 <strong>
                                  Israel Has 
															Been Launching 
															Clandestine Attacks 
															On Iranian Shipping: 
															Report (Updated)
                                 </strong>
                                </font>
                               </a>
                              </font>
                             </p>
